class op4_loop_body:
    var_ranges = {p0: 16, p1: 768}
    index0 = 768*p0 + p1
    index1 = p0
    index2 = p1
    def body(self, ops):
        get_index = self.get_index('index0')
        load = ops.load('buf0', get_index)
        get_index_1 = self.get_index('index1')
        load_1 = ops.load('buf1', get_index_1)
        sub = ops.sub(load, load_1)
        get_index_2 = self.get_index('index1')
        load_2 = ops.load('buf2', get_index_2)
        constant = ops.constant(768.0, torch.float32)
        truediv = ops.truediv(load_2, constant)
        constant_1 = ops.constant(1e-12, torch.float32)
        add = ops.add(truediv, constant_1)
        rsqrt = ops.rsqrt(add)
        mul = ops.mul(sub, rsqrt)
        get_index_3 = self.get_index('index2')
        load_3 = ops.load('arg7_1', get_index_3)
        mul_1 = ops.mul(mul, load_3)
        get_index_4 = self.get_index('index2')
        load_4 = ops.load('arg8_1', get_index_4)
        add_1 = ops.add(mul_1, load_4)
        get_index_5 = self.get_index('index0')
        store = ops.store('buf4', get_index_5, add_1, None)
        return store

    def body(self, ops):
        get_index = self.get_index('index0')
        load = ops.load('arg54_1', get_index)
        get_index_1 = self.get_index('index1')
        load_1 = ops.load('buf63', get_index_1)
        add = ops.add(load, load_1)
        get_index_2 = self.get_index('index1')
        load_2 = ops.load('buf60', get_index_2)
        add_1 = ops.add(add, load_2)
        get_index_3 = self.get_index('index2')
        load_3 = ops.load('buf64', get_index_3)
        sub = ops.sub(add_1, load_3)
        get_index_4 = self.get_index('index2')
        load_4 = ops.load('buf65', get_index_4)

        truediv = ops.truediv(load_4, constant)
        constant_1 = ops.constant(1e-12, torch.float32)
        add_2 = ops.add(truediv, constant_1)
        rsqrt = ops.rsqrt(add_2)
        mul = ops.mul(sub, rsqrt)

        load_5 = ops.load('arg55_1', get_index_5)

    index0 = p1
    index1 = 768*p0 + p1
    index2 = p0
    def body(self, ops):
        get_index = self.get_index('index0')
        load = ops.load('arg102_1', get_index)
        get_index_1 = self.get_index('index1')
        load_1 = ops.load('buf126', get_index_1)
        add = ops.add(load, load_1)
        get_index_2 = self.get_index('index1')
        load_2 = ops.load('buf123', get_index_2)
        add_1 = ops.add(add, load_2)
        get_index_3 = self.get_index('index2')
        load_3 = ops.load('buf127', get_index_3)
        sub = ops.sub(add_1, load_3)
        get_index_4 = self.get_index('index2')
        load_4 = ops.load('buf128', get_index_4)
        constant = ops.constant(768.0, torch.float32)
        truediv = ops.truediv(load_4, constant)
        constant_1 = ops.constant(1e-12, torch.float32)
        add_2 = ops.add(truediv, constant_1)
        rsqrt = ops.rsqrt(add_2)
        mul = ops.mul(sub, rsqrt)
        get_index_5 = self.get_index('index0')
        load_5 = ops.load('arg103_1', get_index_5)

        return store

        get_index_1 = self.get_index('index1')
        load_1 = ops.load('buf231', get_index_1)
        add = ops.add(load, load_1)
        get_index_2 = self.get_index('index1')

        get_index_3 = self.get_index('index2')
